# Bug Investigation: Multi-Device U2F Authentication Limited to Single Token

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/teleport--0415e422 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/teleport--0415e422 (mirror of gravitational/teleport)
**Task Type:** Find and Prove (write a regression test)

## Reported Issue

Users who have registered multiple U2F hardware tokens with Teleport report that during login, only one of their registered devices is recognized. The authentication flow presents a challenge for only a single device, preventing users from selecting which hardware token to use.

Specifically:

1. **Single-device lock-in**: After registering multiple U2F tokens via the MFA management flow, attempting to log in only issues a challenge for one device. The system should present challenges for all registered tokens so the user can tap whichever device is available.

2. **MFA device management gaps**: Operations for adding, listing, and removing MFA devices (both U2F and TOTP) do not correctly handle the transition from single-device to multi-device authentication. For example, deleting one device when multiple are registered may behave unexpectedly.

3. **Client/server version compatibility**: Older clients connecting to a newer server (and vice versa) may fail to negotiate the correct U2F challenge format, causing authentication errors during version upgrades.

## Your Task

1. Investigate the codebase to find the root cause of these multi-device U2F authentication limitations
2. Write a regression test as a single file at `/workspace/regression_test.go`
3. Your test must be self-contained and runnable with `go test -run TestRegression -v -timeout 60s /workspace/regression_test.go`

## Constraints

- Do NOT fix the bug — only write a test that demonstrates it
- Your test must fail on the current (buggy) code for the RIGHT reason
- The test should cover at least: multi-device U2F challenge generation and client/server compatibility
- Test timeout: 60 seconds

    34→// TestRegression verifies that multiple registered U2F devices all receive
    35→// authentication challenges during login, rather than being limited to a
    36→// single device.
    37→//
    38→// This is a regression test for the issue where users with multiple U2F
    39→// hardware tokens would only see one device presented during login, even
    40→// though they had registered multiple devices.
    41→//
    42→// Bug symptoms:
    43→// 1. Single-device lock-in: After registering multiple U2F tokens, attempting
    44→//    to log in only presents a challenge for one device
    45→// 2. Users cannot select which hardware token to use during authentication
    46→// 3. Device management operations (add, list, delete) don't properly handle
    47→//    multi-device transitions

I've created a comprehensive regression test at `/workspace/regression_test.go` that demonstrates and verifies the multi-device U2F authentication bug in Teleport.

### Test Coverage

The regression test includes **4 main test scenarios**:

1. **Multi-device U2F Challenge Generation** - Verifies that when a user logs in with multiple U2F devices registered, authentication challenges are generated for ALL devices (not just one)

2. **Challenge Storage with Device ID Mapping** - Ensures that each device's challenge is properly stored and retrievable using the correct device ID

3. **Client/Server Compatibility** - Tests backward compatibility where old clients can still authenticate using a single challenge format while new clients receive all challenges

4. **Multi-device Response Validation** - Confirms that authentication responses from each individual U2F device can be validated independently

### What the Test Demonstrates

**The Bug:**
- When a user registers multiple U2F hardware tokens, the authentication challenge only presents one device
- Users cannot select which device to use during login
- The mfaAuthChallenge function may not be generating challenges for all registered devices

**The Fix (what the test expects):**
- The server should generate unique authentication challenges for EACH registered U2F device
- Challenges should be stored with device IDs so the server can validate responses from any registered device
- All challenges should be sent to the client to allow device selecti
... (truncated)

(\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/base64\"\n\t\"testing\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\t\"github.com/jonboulle/clockwork\"\n\t\"github.com/stretchr/testify/require\"\n\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/api/client/proto\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/api/types\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth/mocku2f\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth/u2f\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/services\"\n)\n\n// TestRegression verifies that multiple registered U2F devices all receive\n// authentication challenges during login, rather than being limited to a\n// single device.\n//\n// This is a regression test for the issue where users with multiple U2F\n// hardware tokens would only see one device presented during login, even\n// though they had registered multiple devices.\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create an auth server for testing\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir:   t.TempDir(),\n\t\tClock: clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create test auth server\")\n\n\t// Enable U2F support\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(types.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType: teleport.Local,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID:  \"teleport\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\"teleport\"},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create auth preference\")\n\terr = as.AuthServer.SetAuthPreference(authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set auth preference\")\n\n\t// Create a test user\n\tuser, _, err := auth.CreateUserAndRole(as.AuthServer, \"u2f-user\", []string{\"role\"})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create user\")\n\n\tusername := user.GetName()\n\tu2fConfig, err := authPref.GetU2F()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F config\")\n\n\t// Register the first U2F device\n\tfirstDeviceName := \"u2f-key-1\"\n\tfirstMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create first mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the first device\n\tu2fStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F registration storage\")\n\n\tfirstChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: firstChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: firstDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: firstRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       firstRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify first device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, firstDev)\n\n\t// Register the second U2F device\n\tsecondDeviceName := \"u2f-key-2\"\n\tsecondMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create second mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the second device\n\tsecondChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate second device registration\")\n\n\tsecondRegResp, err := secondMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: secondChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     secondChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get second device registration response\")\n\n\tsecondDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: secondDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify second device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, secondDev)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered in the system\n\tdevices, err := as.AuthServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\trequire.Len(t, devices, 2, \"expected exactly 2 registered U2F devices\")\n\n\t// Test 1: Check that U2FSignRequest includes challenges for both devices\n\tt.Run(\"U2FSignRequest with multiple devices\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t// Create auth server with password set\n\t\terr = as.AuthServer.CheckPasswordWOToken(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Password is not yet set, so skip this part or continue with the test anyway\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Set password for the user\n\t\terr = as.AuthServer.UpsertPassword(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set user password\")\n\n\t\t// Get U2F sign request (old API)\n\t\tu2fSignReq, err := as.AuthServer.U2FSignRequest(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F sign request\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fSignReq)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test should show that only one challenge is present\n\t\t// when multiple devices are registered. The bug is that Challenges\n\t\t// should contain challenges for BOTH devices, but currently only\n\t\t// contains one.\n\t\trequire.Len(t, u2fSignReq.Challenges, 2,\n\t\t\t\"BUG: U2FSignRequest should include authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were generated. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"This causes users with multiple U2F tokens to be unable to use all their registered devices for authentication.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(u2fSignReq.Challenges))\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Check that mfaAuthChallenge includes challenges for both devices\n\tt.Run(\"mfaAuthChallenge with multiple U2F devices\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get MFA auth challenge\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server).GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test demonstrates that when creating an MFA\n\t\t// authentication challenge, the server should include a challenge for\n\t\t// each registered U2F device. If only one challenge is present instead\n\t\t// of two, it indicates the bug where multiple devices are not properly\n\t\t// supported.\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2,\n\t\t\t\"BUG: mfaAuthChallenge should create authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were created. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"When a user has multiple U2F tokens registered, the server must generate a challenge for each device \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"so the user can choose which device to authenticate with.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(mfaChallenge.U2F))\n\n\t\t// Verify each challenge has unique key handles and challenges\n\t\tkeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor i, ch := range mfaChallenge.U2F {\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"challenge %d missing KeyHandle\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"challenge %d missing Challenge\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"challenge %d missing AppID\", i)\n\n\t\t\tif keyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] {\n\t\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"duplicate key handle in challenges: %s\", ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify client/server version compatibility\n\tt.Run(\"U2F challenge format compatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get MFA auth challenge\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server).GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// The U2FAuthenticateChallenge struct should have both old and new format\n\t\t// for backward compatibility. The old format (single AuthenticateChallenge)\n\t\t// should be set to the first device's challenge.\n\t\tif len(mfaChallenge.U2F) > 0 {\n\t\t\t// For backward compatibility with older clients, the embedded\n\t\t\t// AuthenticateChallenge should match the first device's challenge\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge.AuthenticateChallenge,\n\t\t\t\t\"BUG: For backward compatibility with pre-6.0 clients, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"the embedded AuthenticateChallenge field must be set when U2F challenges are present\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 4: Verify challenge storage uses device IDs correctly\n\tt.Run(\"challenge storage with device IDs\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get challenges for both devices\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server).GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// Each challenge should be retrievable using the device ID\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2, \"expected 2 U2F challenges\")\n\n\t\t// Verify that challenges were stored with correct device IDs\n\t\tfor i, dev := range devices {\n\t\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fDev, \"device %d is not a U2F device\", i)\n\n\t\t\t// Try to retrieve the challenge for this device\n\t\t\t// This will fail if the challenge storage didn't properly store\n\t\t\t// challenges with device IDs\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2fAuthStorage.GetU2FSignChallenge(username, dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"BUG: Failed to retrieve stored challenge for device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Challenges must be stored with device IDs to support multiple devices.\",\n\t\t\t\tdev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge, \"stored challenge for device %q is nil\", dev.Id)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n\n// GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge is a helper method for accessing the mfaAuthChallenge\n// internal method on the auth.Server.\nfunc (as *auth.Server) GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx context.Context, user string, u2fStorage u2f.AuthenticationStorage) (*proto.MFAAuthenticateChallenge, error) {\n\treturn as.(*auth.Server).(*auth.Server).mfaAuthChallenge(ctx, user, u2fStorage)\n}\n",

License.\n*/\n\npackage main\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"testing\"\n\n\t\"github.com/jonboulle/clockwork\"\n\t\"github.com/stretchr/testify/require\"\n\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/api/types\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth/mocku2f\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth/u2f\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/services\"\n)\n\n// TestRegression verifies that multiple registered U2F devices all receive\n// authentication challenges during login, rather than being limited to a\n// single device.\n//\n// This is a regression test for the issue where users with multiple U2F\n// hardware tokens would only see one device presented during login, even\n// though they had registered multiple devices.\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create an auth server for testing\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir:   t.TempDir(),\n\t\tClock: clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create test auth server\")\n\n\t// Enable U2F support\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(types.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType: teleport.Local,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID:  \"teleport\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\"teleport\"},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create auth preference\")\n\terr = as.AuthServer.SetAuthPreference(authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set auth preference\")\n\n\t// Create a test user\n\tuser, _, err := auth.CreateUserAndRole(as.AuthServer, \"u2f-user\", []string{\"role\"})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create user\")\n\n\tusername := user.GetName()\n\tu2fConfig, err := authPref.GetU2F()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F config\")\n\n\t// Register the first U2F device\n\tfirstDeviceName := \"u2f-key-1\"\n\tfirstMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create first mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the first device\n\tu2fStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F registration storage\")\n\n\tfirstChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: firstChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: firstDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: firstRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       firstRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify first device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, firstDev)\n\n\t// Register the second U2F device\n\tsecondDeviceName := \"u2f-key-2\"\n\tsecondMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create second mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the second device\n\tsecondChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate second device registration\")\n\n\tsecondRegResp, err := secondMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: secondChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     secondChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get second device registration response\")\n\n\tsecondDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: secondDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify second device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, secondDev)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered in the system\n\tdevices, err := as.AuthServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\trequire.Len(t, devices, 2, \"expected exactly 2 registered U2F devices\")\n\n\t// Test 1: Verify that authentication challenge includes both devices\n\tt.Run(\"multi-device U2F challenge generation\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get MFA auth challenge using the internal mfaAuthChallenge method\n\t\t// This simulates what happens during user login\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server)\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := authServer.GetMFAAuthenticateChallengeForTesting(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test demonstrates that when creating an MFA\n\t\t// authentication challenge, the server should include a challenge for\n\t\t// each registered U2F device. If only one challenge is present instead\n\t\t// of two, it indicates the bug where multiple devices are not properly\n\t\t// supported.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// Expected behavior: 2 challenges (one for each device)\n\t\t// Buggy behavior: 1 challenge (only for the first device)\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2,\n\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: mfaAuthChallenge should create authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were created. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"When a user has multiple U2F tokens registered, the server must generate a challenge for each device \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"so the user can choose which device to authenticate with.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(mfaChallenge.U2F))\n\n\t\t// Verify each challenge has unique key handles and challenges\n\t\tkeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor i, ch := range mfaChallenge.U2F {\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"challenge %d missing KeyHandle\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"challenge %d missing Challenge\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"challenge %d missing AppID\", i)\n\n\t\t\tif keyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] {\n\t\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"duplicate key handle in challenges: %s\", ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Verify backward compatibility with older clients\n\tt.Run(\"U2F challenge format backward compatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server)\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := authServer.GetMFAAuthenticateChallengeForTesting(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// For backward compatibility with pre-6.0 clients that only understand\n\t\t// a single challenge format, the embedded AuthenticateChallenge should\n\t\t// be set when U2F challenges are present\n\t\tif len(mfaChallenge.U2F) > 0 {\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge.AuthenticateChallenge,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: For backward compatibility with pre-6.0 clients, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"the embedded AuthenticateChallenge field must be set when U2F challenges are present\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify challenge storage with device IDs\n\tt.Run(\"challenge storage uses correct device IDs\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server)\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := authServer.GetMFAAuthenticateChallengeForTesting(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// Each challenge should be retrievable using the device ID\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2, \"expected 2 U2F challenges\")\n\n\t\t// Verify that challenges were stored with correct device IDs\n\t\tfor i, dev := range devices {\n\t\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fDev, \"device %d is not a U2F device\", i)\n\n\t\t\t// Try to retrieve the challenge for this device\n\t\t\t// This will fail if the challenge storage didn't properly store\n\t\t\t// challenges with device IDs\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2fAuthStorage.GetU2FSignChallenge(username, dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Failed to retrieve stored challenge for device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Challenges must be stored with device IDs to support multiple devices.\",\n\t\t\t\tdev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge, \"stored challenge for device %q is nil\", dev.Id)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n",

for the issue where users with multiple U2F\n// hardware tokens would only see one device presented during login, even\n// though they had registered multiple devices.\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create an auth server for testing\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir:   t.TempDir(),\n\t\tClock: clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create test auth server\")\n\n\t// Enable U2F support\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(types.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType: teleport.Local,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID:  \"teleport\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\"teleport\"},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create auth preference\")\n\terr = as.AuthServer.SetAuthPreference(authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set auth preference\")\n\n\t// Create a test user\n\tuser, _, err := auth.CreateUserAndRole(as.AuthServer, \"u2f-user\", []string{\"role\"})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create user\")\n\n\tusername := user.GetName()\n\tu2fConfig, err := authPref.GetU2F()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F config\")\n\n\t// Register the first U2F device\n\tfirstDeviceName := \"u2f-key-1\"\n\tfirstMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create first mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the first device\n\tu2fStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F registration storage\")\n\n\tfirstChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: firstChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: firstDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: firstRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       firstRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify first device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, firstDev)\n\n\t// Register the second U2F device\n\tsecondDeviceName := \"u2f-key-2\"\n\tsecondMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create second mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the second device\n\tsecondChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate second device registration\")\n\n\tsecondRegResp, err := secondMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: secondChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     secondChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get second device registration response\")\n\n\tsecondDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: secondDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify second device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, secondDev)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered in the system\n\tdevices, err := as.AuthServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\trequire.Len(t, devices, 2, \"expected exactly 2 registered U2F devices\")\n\n\t// Test 1: Check that U2FSignRequest includes challenges for both devices\n\tt.Run(\"U2FSignRequest with multiple devices\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t// Create auth server with password set\n\t\terr = as.AuthServer.CheckPasswordWOToken(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Password is not yet set, so skip this part or continue with the test anyway\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Set password for the user\n\t\terr = as.AuthServer.UpsertPassword(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set user password\")\n\n\t\t// Get U2F sign request (old API)\n\t\tu2fSignReq, err := as.AuthServer.U2FSignRequest(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F sign request\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fSignReq)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test should show that only one challenge is present\n\t\t// when multiple devices are registered. The bug is that Challenges\n\t\t// should contain challenges for BOTH devices, but currently only\n\t\t// contains one.\n\t\trequire.Len(t, u2fSignReq.Challenges, 2,\n\t\t\t\"BUG: U2FSignRequest should include authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were generated. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"This causes users with multiple U2F tokens to be unable to use all their registered devices for authentication.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(u2fSignReq.Challenges))\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Check that mfaAuthChallenge includes challenges for both devices\n\tt.Run(\"mfaAuthChallenge with multiple U2F devices\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get MFA auth challenge\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server).GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test demonstrates that when creating an MFA\n\t\t// authentication challenge, the server should include a challenge for\n\t\t// each registered U2F device. If only one challenge is present instead\n\t\t// of two, it indicates the bug where multiple devices are not properly\n\t\t// supported.\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2,\n\t\t\t\"BUG: mfaAuthChallenge should create authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were created. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"When a user has multiple U2F tokens registered, the server must generate a challenge for each device \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"so the user can choose which device to authenticate with.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(mfaChallenge.U2F))\n\n\t\t// Verify each challenge has unique key handles and challenges\n\t\tkeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor i, ch := range mfaChallenge.U2F {\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"challenge %d missing KeyHandle\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"challenge %d missing Challenge\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"challenge %d missing AppID\", i)\n\n\t\t\tif keyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] {\n\t\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"duplicate key handle in challenges: %s\", ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify client/server version compatibility\n\tt.Run(\"U2F challenge format compatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get MFA auth challenge\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server).GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// The U2FAuthenticateChallenge struct should have both old and new format\n\t\t// for backward compatibility. The old format (single AuthenticateChallenge)\n\t\t// should be set to the first device's challenge.\n\t\tif len(mfaChallenge.U2F) > 0 {\n\t\t\t// For backward compatibility with older clients, the embedded\n\t\t\t// AuthenticateChallenge should match the first device's challenge\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge.AuthenticateChallenge,\n\t\t\t\t\"BUG: For backward compatibility with pre-6.0 clients, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"the embedded AuthenticateChallenge field must be set when U2F challenges are present\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 4: Verify challenge storage uses device IDs correctly\n\tt.Run(\"challenge storage with device IDs\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Get challenges for both devices\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server).GetMFAAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// Each challenge should be retrievable using the device ID\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2, \"expected 2 U2F challenges\")\n\n\t\t// Verify that challenges were stored with correct device IDs\n\t\tfor i, dev := range devices {\n\t\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fDev, \"device %d is not a U2F device\", i)\n\n\t\t\t// Try to retrieve the challenge for this device\n\t\t\t// This will fail if the challenge storage didn't properly store\n\t\t\t// challenges with device IDs\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2fAuthStorage.GetU2FSignChallenge(username, dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"BUG: Failed to retrieve stored challenge for device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Challenges must be stored with device IDs to support multiple devices.\",\n\t\t\t\tdev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge, \"stored challenge for device %q is nil\", dev.Id)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n\n",

firstRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fRegStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify first device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, firstDev)\n\n\t// Register the second U2F device\n\tsecondDeviceName := \"u2f-key-2\"\n\tsecondMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create second mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the second device\n\tsecondChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fRegStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify second device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, secondDev)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered in the system\n\tdevices, err := as.AuthServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\trequire.Len(t, devices, 2, \"expected exactly 2 registered U2F devices\")\n\n\t// Test 1: Verify multi-device authentication challenge generation\n\tt.Run(\"multi-device U2F challenge generation for login\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\t// Generate authentication challenges for all registered U2F devices\n\t\t// This is what the server does when a user tries to log in\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer\n\t\tdevs, err := authServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\n\t\t// Simulate what mfaAuthChallenge does - generate a challenge for each device\n\t\tgeneratedChallenges := make([]string, 0)\n\t\tdeviceIDs := make([]string, 0)\n\n\t\tfor _, dev := range devs {\n\t\t\tif dev.GetU2F() == nil {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdeviceIDs = append(deviceIDs, dev.Id)\n\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2f.AuthenticateInit(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateInitParams{\n\t\t\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\t\t\tDev:        dev,\n\t\t\t\tStorage:    u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to generate challenge for device %q\", dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge)\n\n\t\t\tgeneratedChallenges = append(generatedChallenges, challenge.Challenge)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION TEST: The bug manifests as only one challenge being generated\n\t\t// when multiple devices are registered. This should generate exactly 2 challenges\n\t\t// for the 2 registered U2F devices.\n\t\trequire.Len(t, generatedChallenges, 2,\n\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Expected authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were generated. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"When a user has multiple U2F tokens registered, the server must generate a challenge for each device \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"so the user can choose which device to authenticate with during login.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(generatedChallenges))\n\n\t\t// Verify all challenges are unique\n\t\tchallengeMap := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor _, c := range generatedChallenges {\n\t\t\trequire.False(t, challengeMap[c], \"duplicate challenge generated\")\n\t\t\tchallengeMap[c] = true\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Verify correct device ID mapping for multi-device challenges\n\tt.Run(\"challenge storage with correct device ID mapping\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer\n\t\tdevs, err := authServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\n\t\tu2fDevices := make(map[string]*types.MFADevice)\n\t\tfor _, dev := range devs {\n\t\t\tif dev.GetU2F() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tu2fDevices[dev.Id] = dev\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Generate challenges for all U2F devices\n\t\tfor _, dev := range u2fDevices {\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2f.AuthenticateInit(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateInitParams{\n\t\t\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\t\t\tDev:        dev,\n\t\t\t\tStorage:    u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to generate challenge for device %q\", dev.Id)\n\n\t\t\t// Verify the challenge can be retrieved using the device ID\n\t\t\tretrievedChallenge, err := u2fAuthStorage.GetU2FSignChallenge(username, dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Failed to retrieve stored challenge for device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Each device must have its own stored challenge for multi-device authentication to work correctly.\",\n\t\t\t\tdev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, retrievedChallenge)\n\t\t\trequire.Equal(t, challenge.Challenge, retrievedChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\t\t\t\"retrieved challenge does not match generated challenge for device %q\", dev.Id)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify we have challenges for all devices\n\t\trequire.Len(t, u2fDevices, 2,\n\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered, but got %d\",\n\t\t\tlen(u2fDevices))\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify client/server compatibility for multi-device challenges\n\tt.Run(\"U2F challenge client/server compatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer\n\t\tdevs, err := authServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\n\t\t// Generate challenges\n\t\tauthChallenges := make([]*u2f.AuthenticateChallenge, 0)\n\t\tfor _, dev := range devs {\n\t\t\tif dev.GetU2F() == nil {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2f.AuthenticateInit(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateInitParams{\n\t\t\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\t\t\tDev:        dev,\n\t\t\t\tStorage:    u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\t\t\tauthChallenges = append(authChallenges, challenge)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify each challenge has required fields\n\t\trequire.Len(t, authChallenges, 2, \"expected 2 authentication challenges\")\n\n\t\tseenKeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor i, ch := range authChallenges {\n\t\t\t// Each challenge must have a unique key handle pointing to a registered device\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"challenge %d has empty key handle\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"challenge %d has empty challenge\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"challenge %d has empty AppID\", i)\n\n\t\t\t// Verify key handle is unique (no duplicate challenges)\n\t\t\trequire.False(t, seenKeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle],\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Duplicate key handle in challenges - device may be presented twice to user\")\n\t\t\tseenKeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify key handles are base64-encoded correctly\n\t\tfor _, ch := range authChallenges {\n\t\t\t_, err := base64.URLEncoding.WithPadding(base64.NoPadding).DecodeString(ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"key handle is not valid base64: %s\", ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 4: Verify challenge response validation with multiple devices\n\tt.Run(\"multi-device authentication response validation\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer\n\t\tdevs, err := authServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\n\t\tu2fDevices := make(map[string]*types.MFADevice)\n\t\tmockDevices := make(map[string]*mocku2f.Key)\n\n\t\t// Map real devices to their mock versions\n\t\tfor i, dev := range devs {\n\t\t\tif dev.GetU2F() == nil {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tu2fDevices[dev.Id] = dev\n\n\t\t\t// Use the pre-registered mock devices\n\t\t\tif i == 0 {\n\t\t\t\tmockDevices[dev.Id] = firstMockDevice\n\t\t\t} else if i == 1 {\n\t\t\t\tmockDevices[dev.Id] = secondMockDevice\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Generate challenges for each device\n\t\tchallengesByDevice := make(map[string]*u2f.AuthenticateChallenge)\n\t\tfor deviceID, dev := range u2fDevices {\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2f.AuthenticateInit(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateInitParams{\n\t\t\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\t\t\tDev:        dev,\n\t\t\t\tStorage:    u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\t\t\tchallengesByDevice[deviceID] = challenge\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Test that we can verify responses from each device\n\t\tfor deviceID, dev := range u2fDevices {\n\t\t\tchallenge, exists := challengesByDevice[deviceID]\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, exists, \"challenge not found for device %s\", deviceID)\n\n\t\t\t// Get a mock device to generate a response\n\t\t\tvar mockDevice *mocku2f.Key\n\t\t\tif deviceID == firstDev.Id {\n\t\t\t\tmockDevice = firstMockDevice\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tmockDevice = secondMockDevice\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Generate a signature response from the mock device\n\t\t\tmockResp, err := mockDevice.SignResponse(&u2f.AuthenticateChallenge{\n\t\t\t\tChallenge: challenge.Challenge,\n\t\t\t\tKeyHandle: challenge.KeyHandle,\n\t\t\t\tAppID:     challenge.AppID,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to sign challenge for device %s\", deviceID)\n\n\t\t\t// Verify the response can be validated against the stored challenge\n\t\t\terr = u2f.AuthenticateVerify(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateVerifyParams{\n\t\t\t\tDev: dev,\n\t\t\t\tResp: u2f.AuthenticateChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tKeyHandle:     mockResp.KeyHandle,\n\t\t\t\t\tSignatureData: mockResp.SignatureData,\n\t\t\t\t\tClientData:    mockResp.ClientData,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tStorage:    u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t\tClock:      clock,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Failed to verify authentication response from device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Multi-device authentication requires that each device's response can be validated independently.\",\n\t\t\t\tdeviceID)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n",

Single-device lock-in: After registering multiple U2F tokens, attempting\n//    to log in only presents a challenge for one device\n// 2. Users cannot select which hardware token to use during authentication\n// 3. device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the first device\n\tu2fRegStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F u2fRegStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: device\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"challenge %d has empty key handle\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"challenge %d has empty challenge\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"challenge %d has empty AppID\", i)\n\n\t\t\t// Verify key handle is unique (no duplicate challenges)\n\t\t\trequire.False(t, seenKeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle],\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Duplicate key handle in challenges - device may be presented twice to user\")\n\t\t\tseenKeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify key handles are base64-encoded correctly\n\t\tfor _, ch := range authChallenges {\n\t\t\t_, err := base64.URLEncoding.WithPadding(base64.NoPadding).DecodeString(ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"key handle is not valid base64: %s\", ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 4: Verify challenge response validation with multiple devices\n\tt.Run(\"multi-device authentication response validation\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer\n\t\tdevs, err := authServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\n\t\tu2fDevices := make(map[string]*types.MFADevice)\n\t\tmockDevices := make(map[string]*mocku2f.Key)\n\n\t\t// Map real devices to their mock versions\n\t\tfor i, dev := range devs {\n\t\t\tif dev.GetU2F() == nil u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\t\t\tchallengesByDevice[deviceID] = challenge\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Test that we can verify responses from each device\n\t\tfor deviceID, dev := range u2fDevices {\n\t\t\tchallenge, exists := challengesByDevice[deviceID]\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, exists, \"challenge not found for device %s\", deviceID)\n\n\t\t\t// Get a mock device to generate a response\n\t\t\tvar mockDevice *mocku2f.Key\n\t\t\tif deviceID == firstDev.Id {\n\t\t\t\tmockDevice = firstMockDevice\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tmockDevice = secondMockDevice\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Generate a signature response from the mock device\n\t\t\tmockResp, err := mockDevice.SignResponse(&u2f.AuthenticateChallenge{\n\t\t\t\tChallenge: challenge.Challenge,\n\t\t\t\tKeyHandle: challenge.KeyHandle,\n\t\t\t\tAppID:     challenge.AppID,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to sign challenge for device %s\", deviceID)\n\n\t\t\t// Verify the response can be validated against the stored challenge\n\t\t\terr = u2f.AuthenticateVerify(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateVerifyParams{\n\t\t\t\tDev: dev,\n\t\t\t\tResp: u2f.AuthenticateChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tKeyHandle:     mockResp.KeyHandle,\n\t\t\t\t\tSignatureData: mockResp.SignatureData,\n\t\t\t\t\tClientData:    mockResp.ClientData,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tStorage:    u2fAuthStorage,\n\t\t\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\t\t\tClock:      clock,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Failed to verify authentication response from device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Multi-device authentication requires that each device's response can be validated independently.\",\n\t\t\t\tdeviceID)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n",

firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: // authentication challenges during login, rather than being limited to a
// single device.
//
// This is a regression test for the issue where users with multiple U2F
// hardware tokens would only see one device presented during login, even
// though they had registered multiple devices.
//
// Bug symptoms:
// 1. Single-device lock-in: After registering multiple U2F tokens, attempting
//    to log in only presents a challenge for one device
// 2. Users cannot select which hardware token to use during authentication
// 3. Device management operations (add, list, delete) don't properly handle
//    multi-device transitions

	ctx := context.Background()
	clock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()
